      70             : char *TTFFoundry=NULL;
      71             : 
      72             : /* This file produces a ttf file given a splinefont. */
      73             : 
      74             : /* ************************************************************************** */
      75             : 
      76             : /* Required tables:
      77             :         cmap            encoding
      78             :         head            header data
      79             :         hhea            horizontal metrics header data
      80             :         hmtx            horizontal metrics (widths, lsidebearing)
      81             :         maxp            various maxima in the font
      82             :         name            various names associated with the font
      83             :         post            postscript names and other stuff
      84             : Required by windows but not mac
      85             :         OS/2            bleah.
      86             : Required for TrueType
      87             :         loca            pointers to the glyphs
      88             :         glyf            character shapes
      89             : Required for OpenType (PostScript)
      90             :         CFF             A complete postscript CFF font here with all its internal tables
      91             : Required for bitmaps
      92             :         bdat/EBDT       bitmap data
      93             :         bloc/EBLC       pointers to bitmaps
      94             :         bhed            for apple bitmap only fonts, replaces head
      95             : Optional for bitmaps
      96             :         EBSC            bitmap scaling table (used in windows "bitmap-only" fonts)
      97             : "Advanced Typograpy"
      98             :   Apple
      99             :         feat            (mapping between morx features and 'name' names)
     100             :         kern            (if data are present)
     101             :         lcar            (ligature caret, if data present)
     102             :         morx            (substitutions, if data present)
     103             :         prop            (glyph properties, if data present)
     104             :         opbd            (optical bounds, if data present)
     105             :   OpenType
     106             :         GPOS            (opentype, if kern,anchor data are present)
     107             :         GSUB            (opentype, if ligature (other subs) data are present)
     108             :         GDEF            (opentype, if anchor data are present)
     109             : MATH
     110             :         MATH            (MS proposal, if math data present)
     111             : Apple variation tables (for distortable (multiple master type) fonts)
     112             :         fvar            (font variations)
     113             :         gvar            (glyph variations)
     114             :         cvar            (cvt variations)
     115             :         avar            (axis variations)
     116             : additional tables
     117             :         cvt             for hinting
     118             :         gasp            to control when things should be hinted
     119             :         fpgm            for hinting (currently only copied and dumped verbatim)
     120             :         prep            for hinting (currently only copied and dumped verbatim)
     121             : FontForge
     122             :         PfEd            My own table
     123             : TeX
     124             :         TeX             TeX specific info (stuff that used to live in tfm files)
     125             : */
